  <script>
	;(function () {
		var w = typeof window != 'undefined' ? window : exports,
				entries = [];
		w.performance || (w.performance = {});
		w.performance.now || (
				w.performance.now = performance.now || performance.webkitNow ||
				performance.msNow || performance.mozNow);
		if (!w.performance.now){
			var s = Date.now ? Date.now() : +(new Date());
			if  (w.performance.timing && w.performance.timing.navigationStart)
				s = performance.timing.navigationStart;
			w.performance.now = (function(){
				var n = Date.now ? Date.now() : +(new Date());
				return n-s;
			});
		}

		w.performance.mark || (
				w.performance.mark =
						w.performance.webkitMark ? w.performance.webkitMark :
								(function (l) {
									entries.forEach(function(e, i, a){
										if (e.name === l) a.splice(i,1);
									});
									entries.push({'name':l,'entryType':'mark','startTime':w.performance.now(),'duration':0});
								}));

		w.performance.getEntriesByType || (
				w.performance.getEntriesByType =
						w.performance.webkitGetEntriesByType ? w.performance.webkitGetEntriesByType :
								(function (t) {
									var filter = function(el){return el.entryType === t};
									return ['mark', 'measure'].indexOf(t) !== -1 ? entries.filter(filter) : undefined;
								}));

		w.performance.getEntriesByName || (
				w.performance.getEntriesByName =
						w.performance.webkitGetEntriesByName ? w.performance.webkitGetEntriesByName :
								(function (n) {
									return entries.filter(function(el){return el.name === n});
								}));

		w.performance.clearMeasures || (
				w.performance.clearMeasures =
						w.performance.webkitClearMeasures ? w.performance.webkitClearMeasures :
								(function (n) {
									entries.forEach(function(e, i, a){
										if (e.entryType === 'measure') a.splice(i,1);
									});
									entries = [];
								}));

		w.performance.clearMarks || (
				w.performance.clearMarks =
						w.performance.webkitClearMarks ? w.performance.webkitClearMarks :
								(function (n) {
									entries.forEach(function(e, i, a){
										if (e.entryType === 'mark') a.splice(i,1);
									});
									entries = [];
								}));

		w.performance.measure || (
				w.performance.measure =
						w.performance.webkitMeasure ? w.performance.webkitMeasure :
								(function (n, s, e) {
									var filter = function(comp){return function(el){return el.name === comp && el.entryType === 'mark'}},
											sMark = entries.filter(filter(s))[0],
											eMark = entries.filter(filter(e))[0],
											dur   = eMark.startTime - sMark.startTime;
									entries.push({'name': n, 'entryType' : 'measure', 'startTime': sMark.startTime, 'duration': dur });
								}));
	}());
	(function() {
		var unsentEvents = [];

		var wtt = function(n, t, b) {
			t = Math.round(t);
			if (t >= 0 && t < 3600000 && !b) {
				// Google Analytics
				if (window['_gaq']) {
					_gaq.push(['_trackTiming', 'UserTimings', n, t]);
				}

				var flowPerformanceImprovementsVariant = '';

				
					// Mixpanel

					var event = { name: n, timing: t };

					var trackRUMEventWithMixpanel = function (e) {
						mixpanel.track('RUM - ' + e.name, {
							timing: e.timing,
							flowPerformanceImprovementsVariant: flowPerformanceImprovementsVariant
						});
					};

					if (window['mixpanel']) {
						if (unsentEvents.length) {
							unsentEvents.forEach(trackRUMEventWithMixpanel);
							unsentEvents = [];
						}
						trackRUMEventWithMixpanel(event);
					} else {
						unsentEvents.push(event);
					}
				
			}
		};

		window.markUserTime = function(l) {
			var raf = window['requestAnimationFrame'] ||
				(function(callback){setTimeout(callback, 0);});
			raf(function(){
				if (!window.performance || !window.performance.mark) {
					return;
				}

				window.performance.mark(l);

				if (window['console'] && console['timeStamp'])
					console.timeStamp(l);

				var mark = window.performance.getEntriesByName(l)[0];
				wtt(mark.name, mark.startTime, false);
			});
		};
	})();
</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
	config.landingCalculatorView = 'landingCalculator';
	config.calculatorSourceCurrency = "";
	config.calculatorTargetCurrency = "";

  <script type="text/javascript">

	var chartUrl = "/landing/historicRates?monthRate=true";

	var rateMessageUrl = "/landing/getExchangeRateMessage";

		var RateHistoryChart = function(currentPairHistory, url, rateMessageUrl){
			this.currentPairHistory = currentPairHistory || [];
			this.forceUpdate = false;
			this.ctx = document.getElementById("b-exchange-chart__canvas").getContext("2d");
			this.grd = this.ctx.createLinearGradient(0.000, 150.000, 300.000, 150.000);

			//Colours for chart line's gradient
			this.grd.addColorStop(0.002, 'rgba(0, 185, 255, 1.000)');
			this.grd.addColorStop(0.204, 'rgba(13, 189, 226, 1.000)');
			this.grd.addColorStop(0.492, 'rgba(30, 195, 191, 1.000)');
			this.grd.addColorStop(0.695, 'rgba(30, 195, 191, 1.000)');
			this.grd.addColorStop(0.897, 'rgba(69, 210, 108, 1.000)');
			this.grd.addColorStop(1.000, 'rgba(88, 217, 67, 1.000)');

			this.chartBlock = jQuery('.b-exchange-chart');
			this.chartSourceCur = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__chart-from');
			this.chartTargetCur = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__chart-to');
			this.chartRate = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__rate');
			this.mainRateMessage = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__rate-message-main');
			this.defaultRateMessage = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__rate-message-main').html();
			this.floatingRateMessage = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__rate-message-floating');
			this.fixedRateMessage = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__rate-message-fixed');
			this.fixedRateExpiryHours = this.fixedRateMessage.find('.hours');
			this.chartPeriodTitle = this.chartBlock.find('#chartPeriodTitle');

			this.calcSourceCur = 'GBP';
			this.calcTargetCur = 'EUR';
			
			this.currenciesWithRateProvidersNotDisplayed = ["NGN"]
			

			this.rateLinks = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__see-links');
			this.xeLink = this.chartBlock.find('a.b-exchange-chart__compare-link-xe');
			this.googleLink = this.chartBlock.find('a.b-exchange-chart__compare-link-google');
			this.yahooLink = this.chartBlock.find('a.b-exchange-chart__compare-link-yahoo');

			this.rateAlertLink = this.chartBlock.find('a.b-exchange-chart__rate-alerts-link');

			this.loadSpinner = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__rate-spinner');
			this.loadingText = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__loading-text');
			this.chartHeader = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__chartHeader');
			this.rateAlertCta = this.chartBlock.find('.b-exchange-chart__rate-alerts-cta');

			this.url = url;
			this.rateMessageUrl = rateMessageUrl;

			this.chartOptions = {
				responsive: true,
				///Boolean - Whether grid lines are shown across the chart
				scaleShowGridLines : true,
				//Boolean - Whether to show horizontal lines (except X axis)
				scaleShowHorizontalLines: true,
				//Boolean - Whether to show vertical lines (except Y axis)
				scaleShowVerticalLines: false,
				//Boolean - Whether the line is curved between points
				bezierCurve : true,
				//Number - Tension of the bezier curve between points
				bezierCurveTension : 0.1,
				//Boolean - Whether to show a dot for each point
				pointDot : false,
				 //Number - Radius of each point dot in pixels
				pointDotRadius : 5,
				//Number - Pixel width of point dot stroke
				pointDotStrokeWidth : 2,
				//Number - amount extra to add to the radius to cater for hit detection outside the drawn point
				pointHitDetectionRadius : 20,
				//Boolean - Whether to fill the dataset with a colour
				datasetFill : false,
				//String - A legend template
				legendTemplate : "",
				// Boolean - Whether to animate the chart
				animation: true,
				//Number - Pixel width of dataset stroke
				datasetStrokeWidth : 4,
				// Boolean - If we should show the scale at all
				showScale: true,
				// String - Colour of the scale line
				scaleLineColor: "#e2e6e8",
				// Number - Pixel width of the scale line
				scaleLineWidth: 1,
				// Boolean - Whether to show labels on the scale
				scaleShowLabels: true,
				// String - Scale label font declaration for the scale label
				scaleFontFamily: "'Helvetica Neue', 'Helvetica', 'Arial', sans-serif",
				// Number - Scale label font size in pixels
				scaleFontSize: 12,
				// String - Scale label font weight style
				scaleFontStyle: "normal",
				// String - Scale label font colour
				scaleFontColor: "#829ca9",
				// Boolean - Determines whether to draw tooltips on the canvas or not
				showTooltips: false
			};

			this.lineChartData = {
				labels : [],
				datasets : [
					{
						fillColor : "rgba(151,187,205,0.2)",
						strokeColor : this.grd,
						pointColor : "#00B9FF",
						pointStrokeColor : "#fff",
						pointHighlightFill : "#fff",
						pointHighlightStroke : "rgba(151,187,205,1)",
						data : []
					}
				]
			};

			this.init();
		};

		RateHistoryChart.prototype = {
			init: function() {
				var self = this;
				self.createChart();
			},

			createChart: function() {
				this.createOrUpdateIfRequired();
			},

			createOrUpdateIfRequired: function(forceUpdate, transferEstimate) {
				var self = this;
				if (typeof self.currentPairHistory == "undefined" || self.isEmpty(self.currentPairHistory) || forceUpdate) {
					self.loadSpinner.show();
					$.ajax({
						url : self.url,
						type: "POST",
						data : {
						source: self.calcSourceCur,
							target: self.calcTargetCur
						},
						success: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
							self.currentPairHistory = data;
							self.updateDataSet();
							self.updateOrCreateChart(transferEstimate);
							self.forceUpdate = false;
						},
						error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
							console.log(errorThrown);
						}
					});
				} else {
					self.updateDataSet();
					self.updateOrCreateChart();
				}

				return self.currentPairHistory;
			},

			updateDataSet: function() {
				var self = this;
				if (!self.currentPairHistory.rates) return;

				var labels = [];
				for (var i = 0; i < self.currentPairHistory.rates.length; i++) {
					labels.push("   ");
				}
				self.lineChartData.labels = labels;
				self.lineChartData.datasets[0].data = self.currentPairHistory.rates;

				return self.lineChartData
			},

			updateOrCreateChart: function(transferEstimate) {
				var self = this;
				if (self.myLine) {
					self.myLine.destroy();
					self.myLine = new Chart(self.ctx).Line(self.lineChartData, self.chartOptions)
				} else {
					self.myLine = new Chart(self.ctx).Line(self.lineChartData, self.chartOptions);
				}

				self.chartSourceCur.text(self.currentPairHistory.pair.sourceCurrency);
				self.chartTargetCur.text(self.currentPairHistory.pair.targetCurrency);
				self.updateCurrentRate(self.currentPairHistory.rates[self.currentPairHistory.rates.length - 1]);
				self.chartPeriodTitle.text(self.currentPairHistory.periodTitle);
				self.loadingText.hide();
				self.chartHeader.show();
				self.loadSpinner.hide();
				self.rateAlertCta.show();
				self.updateComparisonLinks();
				self.updateRateAlertLink();
				self.hideRateProviderDisplayIfCurrencyExcluded(self.calcTargetCur);
				self.getExchangeRateMessage(transferEstimate);
			},

			//This method is deprecated
			updateIfCurrencyChanged: function(source, target) {
				this.calcSourceCur = source;
				this.calcTargetCur = target;

				this.createOrUpdateIfRequired(true);
			},

			updateOnCurrencyChanged: function(currencyChangedModel) {
				this.calcSourceCur = currencyChangedModel.sourceCurrencyCode;
				this.calcTargetCur = currencyChangedModel.targetCurrencyCode;

				this.createOrUpdateIfRequired(true, currencyChangedModel.transferEstimate);
			},

			updateComparisonLinks: function() {
				var self = this;
				var xeRangeParam = "";
				if (self.currentPairHistory.periodTitle.indexOf("30") >= 0) {
					xeRangeParam = "&view=1M";
				} else {
					xeRangeParam = ""
				}

				this.xeLink.attr("href", "http://www.xe.com/currencycharts/?from=" + self.currentPairHistory.pair.sourceCurrency +"&to=" + self.currentPairHistory.pair.targetCurrency + xeRangeParam);
				this.googleLink.attr("href", "https://www.google.co.uk/finance?q=" + self.currentPairHistory.pair.sourceCurrency + self.currentPairHistory.pair.targetCurrency);
				this.yahooLink.attr("href", "https://uk.finance.yahoo.com/q?s=" + self.currentPairHistory.pair.sourceCurrency + self.currentPairHistory.pair.targetCurrency + "=X");
			},

			updateRateAlertLink: function() {
				this.rateAlertLink.attr("href", "https://transferwise.com/tools/exchange-rate-alerts?utm_source=transferwise&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=rate_chart/#subscribe?fromCurrency=" + this.currentPairHistory.pair.sourceCurrency + "&toCurrency=" + this.currentPairHistory.pair.targetCurrency);
			},

			isEmpty: function(myObject) {
				for(var key in myObject) {
					if (myObject.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
						return false;
					}
				}
				return true;
			},

			updateCurrentRate: function(rate) {
			  this.chartRate.text(rate);
			},

			//This method is deprecated
			updateRateMessage: function(isFixedRate, fixedRateExpiryHours) {
				if(isFixedRate) {
					this.fixedRateExpiryHours.html(fixedRateExpiryHours);
					this.fixedRateMessage.show();
					this.floatingRateMessage.hide();
				} else {
					this.fixedRateMessage.hide();
					this.floatingRateMessage.show();
				}
			},

			hideRateProviderDisplayIfCurrencyExcluded : function(currency){
				var self = this;
				var isCurrencyExcluded = self.isCurrencyRateDisplayExcluded(currency);
				if(isCurrencyExcluded){
					self.rateLinks.hide();
				}else{
					self.rateLinks.show();
				}
			},

			isCurrencyRateDisplayExcluded : function(currency){
				var self = this;
				var excludedCurrencies = self.currenciesWithRateProvidersNotDisplayed;
				for(var i = 0; i < excludedCurrencies.length; i++){
					if(currency == excludedCurrencies[i]){
						return true;
					}
				}
				return false;
			},

			getExchangeRateMessage: function(transferEstimate) {
				var self = this;
				$.ajax({
						url : self.rateMessageUrl +"?currency=" + self.calcTargetCur,
						type: "GET",
						data : {},
						success: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
							self.updateExchangeRateMessage(data.message, transferEstimate);
						},
						error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
							console.log(errorThrown);
						}
					});
			},

			updateExchangeRateMessage : function(currencyRateMessageFromConfig, transferEstimate){
				var self = this;

				if(currencyRateMessageFromConfig){
					self.mainRateMessage.html(currencyRateMessageFromConfig);
				}else{
					self.mainRateMessage.html(self.defaultRateMessage);
				}

				if(transferEstimate){
					if(transferEstimate.isFixedRate) {
						this.fixedRateExpiryHours.html(transferEstimate.fixedRateExpiryHours);
						this.fixedRateMessage.show();
						this.floatingRateMessage.hide();
					} else {
						this.fixedRateMessage.hide();
						if(!currencyRateMessageFromConfig){
							this.floatingRateMessage.show();
						}else{
							this.floatingRateMessage.hide();
						}
					}
				}else{
					this.fixedRateMessage.hide();
					this.floatingRateMessage.hide();
				}
			}
		};

		var v = {"pair":{"sourceCurrency":"GBP","targetCurrency":"EUR"},"rates":[1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.322485,1.328485,1.352785,1.332485,1.382485,1.322485,1.322485]};
		$(function(){
			rateHistoryChart = new RateHistoryChart({}, chartUrl, rateMessageUrl);
		});

		jQuery('.js-chart-compare-link').click(function () {
			var provider = $(this).data('provider');
		});

</script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
	$(function() {
		var CurrencyWishesHandler = function(block, openCWOnStart) {
			this.block = block;
			this.openCWOnStart = openCWOnStart;
			this.curFromSelect = this.block.find('select[name="currencyFrom"]');
			this.curToSelect = this.block.find('select[name="currencyTo"]');
			this.closePopUpLink = this.block.find('a#close-cur-wish-pop');
			this.firePopUpLink = this.block.find('a#fire-cur-wish-pop');
			this.curWishListForm = this.block.find('#curWishListForm');
			this.addFriendsForm = this.block.find('#addFriendsForm');
			this.submitStep1 = this.block.find('input.submit-curr-wish');
			this.submitStep2 = this.block.find('input.submit-add-friends');
			this.init();
		};

		CurrencyWishesHandler.prototype = {
			init: function() {
				var self = this;
				this.activeForm = "initial";

				this.closePopUpLink.click(function() {
					$.fancybox.close();
					LogUtils.sendGoogleAnalyticsEvent('CurrencyWishesPopUp', self.activeForm + '-screen-click-close');

					self.resetDialog();
				});

				this.firePopUpLink.fancybox({
					'showCloseButton': false,
					'hideOnOverlayClick' : false,
					'overlayOpacity': 0.5,
					padding: 0,
					onStart: function(){
						$("#fancybox-outer, #fancybox-bg-n, #fancybox-bg-ne, #fancybox-bg-e, #fancybox-bg-se," +
								"#fancybox-bg-s, #fancybox-bg-sw, #fancybox-bg-w, #fancybox-bg-nw").css("background","none");
					}
				});

				this.submitStep1.click(function(e) {
					e.preventDefault();

					var subheadText = self.addFriendsForm.find('.add-friends-subhead').html();

					var currencyFrom = self.curFromSelect.val();
					var currencyTo = self.curToSelect.val();
					var errors = self.curWishListForm.find('.errors');

					$.ajax({
						type: "POST",
						url: "/currencyWishes/captureCurrencyWish",
						dataType: "json",
						data: self.curWishListForm.serialize(),
						success: function (result) {
							errors.hide();

							if (result.redirectToPaymentFlow) {
								window.location.href = result.redirectToPaymentFlow;
							}

							if (result.success) {
								// self.addFriendsForm.find('.add-friends-subhead').html(Mustache.render(subheadText, {currencyFrom: currencyFrom, currencyTo: currencyTo}));

								self.curWishListForm.hide();
								self.addFriendsForm.show();
								self.activeForm = "final"
							} else {
								if (result.errors) {
									errors.html(self.parseErrorList(result.errors));
									errors.show();
								}
							}
						}
					});

					LogUtils.sendGoogleAnalyticsEvent('CurrencyWishesPopUp', 'initial-screen-all-done-click');
					return false;
				});

				this.submitStep2.click(function(e) {
					e.preventDefault();

					var currencyFrom = self.curFromSelect.val();
					var currencyTo = self.curToSelect.val();
					var emailsInput = self.addFriendsForm.find('#emailsInput');
					var message = self.addFriendsForm.find('.message');
					var errors = self.addFriendsForm.find('.errors');

					$.ajax({
						type: "POST",
						url: "/currencyWishes/addFriends",
						dataType: "json",
						data: self.addFriendsForm.serialize() + "&currencyFrom=" + currencyFrom + "&currencyTo=" + currencyTo,
						success: function (result) {
							message.hide();
							errors.hide();
							emailsInput.val('');

							if (result.success && result.message) {
								message.show();
								message.text(result.message);
							}

							if (result.errors) {
								errors.html(self.parseErrorList(result.errors));
								errors.show();
							}
						}
					});

					LogUtils.sendGoogleAnalyticsEvent('CurrencyWishesPopUp', 'final-screen-add-friends-to-the-list-click');
					return false;
				});

				this.openCWOnStartIfRequired();
			},

			resetDialog: function() {
				this.curWishListForm[0].reset();
				this.activeForm = "initial";
				this.addFriendsForm.hide();
				this.curWishListForm.show();
			},

			parseErrorList: function(errors) {
				var result = '';
				$.each(errors, function (index, value) {
					result += value + "</br>";
				});

				return result;
			},

			openCWOnStartIfRequired: function() {
				var self = this;

				if (self.openCWOnStart) {
					self.firePopUpLink.click();
				}
			}

		};
		new CurrencyWishesHandler(jQuery('#cur-wish-dialog'), false);
	});
</script>

	function extend(obj, src) {
		for (var key in src) {
			if (src.hasOwnProperty(key)) obj[key] = src[key];
		}
		return obj;
	}
